[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark BER [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBasic[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEncoding Rules[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m dissector. The issue occurs in the `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction when processing BER-encoded data, resulting in a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write operation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat overflows a stack-allocated buffer named `name_string`. This vulnerability was[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdiscovered through fuzzing using the `handler_ber` fuzzer with AddressSanitizer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstrumentation.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as an AddressSanitizer-detected stack-buffer-overflow with a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m, classified as a [0m[32m"1-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow"[0m[39m. The [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability occurs during the dissection of BER-encoded packets when the fuzzer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutes a test case through the `handler_ber` fuzzer.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerability Details:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack-buffer-overflow occurs at the following location:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **File**: `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-ber.c[0m[39m`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Function**: `dissect_ber_GeneralString`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line**: [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m34[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Operation**: WRITE of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Address**: `[0m[1;36m0x7ffd3b4e7a3f[0m[39m`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Call Stack Analysis:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following execution path:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer entry point `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` initiates packet dissection[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Through the standard Wireshark dissection chain [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`epan_dissect_run` → [0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow affects a variable in the `try_dissect_unknown_ber` function's stack [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mframe:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function contains [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m stack-allocated objects[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The problematic buffer `name_string` is allocated at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m240[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize of [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The memory access occurs at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m, which is one byte before the start of the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string` buffer[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This indicates an underflow condition where data is written just before the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended buffer boundary[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m147:e[0m[39mxtern int [0m[1;35mdissect_ber_GeneralString[0m[1;39m([0m[39masn1_ctx_t *actx, proto_tree *tree, [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I have identified the root[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability in the `dissect_ber_GeneralString`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe current implementation of `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3172[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3199[0m[39m in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m contains two critical bugs:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Bug #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3188[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Reading from Wrong Buffer:**[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code reads `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` from the original `tvb`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer at the current `offset`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After `dissect_ber_restricted_string` returns, the `offset` has advanced past [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe BER-encoded string data[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function should instead read the length from `out_tvb`, which contains the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed string content as a subset buffer created by `dissect_ber_restricted_string`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reading from the wrong location causes `tvb_len` to contain arbitrary/garbage [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata from the packet[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Bug #[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3194[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Buffer Overflow:**[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code writes `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;` without proper bounds checking[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `tvb_len >= name_len` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., both equal [0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this writes to [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which is one byte past the end of the [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalid [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindices are [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m79[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is the direct cause of the stack-buffer-overflow detected by [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evidence from Code Analysis[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe disabled old implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3040[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3101[0m[39m, wrapped in `#if [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m #endif`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshows the correct pattern:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3090[0m[39m: Clamps the length before copying: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m len[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m= max_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m3094[0m[39m: Safely writes the null terminator: `str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe old implementation correctly ensured that the null terminator was always [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwritten within buffer bounds by reserving space for it.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Data Flow Understanding[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `dissect_ber_GeneralString` calls `dissect_ber_restricted_string` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3179[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This eventually creates `out_tvb` as a subset of the original tvb containing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjust the string data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1780[0m[39m in `dissect_ber_constrained_octet_string_impl`[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The correct length should be obtained from `out_tvb` using [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;35mtvb_captured_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Before indexing into `name_string`, the length must be clamped to ensure it's [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mless than `name_len`[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix Location[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** `epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Function:** `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3172[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3199[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Specific Changes Required[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix Line [0m[1;36m3188[0m[39m - Correct Length Retrieval**[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis ensures we get the actual length of the parsed string data from `out_tvb` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of reading arbitrary data from the wrong buffer location.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix Line [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m - Add Bounds Checking**[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBefore line [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m, add a bounds check to clamp `tvb_len`:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tvb_len = name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOr more concisely, replace the section from lines [0m[1;36m3188[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m with:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mname_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Variable Type Correction**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange the type of `tvb_len` from `int8_t` to `unsigned` to match the return type [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and avoid potential signed/unsigned comparison issues:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned tvb_len;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Details[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe complete fixed implementation should look like:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mNOLINTNEXTLINE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmisc-no-recursion[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mdissect_ber_GeneralString[0m[1;39m([0m[39masn1_ctx_t *actx, proto_tree *tree, tvbuff_t *tvb, int [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset, int hf_id, char *name_string, unsigned name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tvbuff_t *out_tvb = NULL;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    unsigned tvb_len;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Changed from int8_t[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    offset = [0m[1;35mdissect_ber_restricted_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse, BER_UNI_TAG_GeneralString, actx, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtree, tvb, offset, hf_id, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? &out_tvb : NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         * XXX - do we want to just get what's left in the tvbuff[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         * if the full length isn't available in the tvbuff, or[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         * do we want to throw an exception?[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Fixed: get length from [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect buffer[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                tvb_len = name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Clamp for null terminator[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Now safe: tvb_len < name_len [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguaranteed[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return offset;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses Both Root Causes:** The fix corrects both the incorrect buffer read [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the buffer overflow condition[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Patterns:** The fix mirrors the approach used in the old, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3094[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which successfully prevented buffer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflows by clamping the length before writing the null terminator[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Changes:** The fix requires only modifying a few lines in one [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction, reducing the risk of introducing new bugs[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves Function Behavior:** The fix maintains the same API contract and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior expected by callers like `try_dissect_unknown_ber` at line [0m[1;36m935[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Type Safety:** Changing `tvb_len` from `int8_t` to `unsigned` prevents [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotential overflow issues with signed byte values and matches the return type of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **API Compatibility:** The function signature remains unchanged, so all existing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcallers continue to work without modification[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Dissection Logic:** The BER parsing logic via `dissect_ber_restricted_string` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis unchanged; only the string copying and null termination logic is fixed[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Optional Parameter Handling:** The conditional handling of `name_string` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`out_tvb` pointers remains the same[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Return Value:** The function still returns the correct offset value for [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinued parsing[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report Issues[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fixes the Stack-Buffer-Overflow:** By clamping `tvb_len` to be less than [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_len` before indexing, the write to `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` is guaranteed to be[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin bounds[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Eliminates Arbitrary Data Read:** By reading from `out_tvb` instead of the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal `tvb` at the wrong offset, the length value is now correct and [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeterministic[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Handles Edge Cases:** When `tvb_len >= name_len`, the code now correctly [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopies only `name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes and places the null terminator at [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mname_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, preventing any overflow[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Addresses the Fuzzer Test Case:** The specific test case that triggered the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith approximately [0m[1;36m213[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now be handled safely, with [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproper bounds checking preventing the overflow[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **String Truncation:** When the parsed BER GeneralString is longer than the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovided buffer, it will now be truncated. This is the correct and safe behavior, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching the old implementation's approach.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance:** The fix has negligible performance impact, adding only a simple[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomparison and assignment operation.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Compatibility:** The fix maintains full backward compatibility with all [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting callers and does not change the function's external behavior in valid use [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcases.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe disabled old implementation at lines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3094[0m[39m demonstrates the exact same [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    len = max_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, str, offset, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstr[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis validates that the clamping approach is the established pattern in this [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase for preventing buffer overflows when copying strings with null [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtermination.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
